   <!-- AGE 3 UNIT ACTIONS -->
      <!-- The DamageDefensesAttack here is compared to the target's Defense, which provides a value to use to scale damage.  So, a 7 DamageDefensesAttack on this ability vs. a Palisade with 7 Defense is 7 / 7 = 1 or 100%.  The Catpult has .75 DamageDefensesStrength, so with the 1 scaling we get 100% of that, meaning that the wall takes the full .75 and is 75% damaged / 25% remaining.

      The same attack against a Stone Wall, with 20 Defense, is 7 / 20 = .35.  In this case, the Catapult's .75 is scaled by the .35, so .75 * .35 = .2625.  The Stone Wall should be at 73.75% HP remaining after one Catapult Siege Unit Ability .-->


      <ACard>
         <ID>UNITACTIONS-SIEGE_DAMAGEDEFENSES</ID>
         <CardSpriteName>UI/Icons/Unit Actions/SIEGE_DEFENSES</CardSpriteName>
         <ExecutionType>CX_All</ExecutionType>
         <Choices>
            <ACardChoice>
               <Requirements>
                  <ACardRequirement>
                     <ReqType>CR_GameData</ReqType>
                     <Req>MovedThisTurn,BOOL_FALSE,0</Req>
                     <UseBooleanFormat>true</UseBooleanFormat>
                     <UsePlainFormat>true</UsePlainFormat>
                  </ACardRequirement>
                  <!-- <ACardRequirement>
                     <ReqType>CR_EntityTagCount</ReqType>
                     <Req>HOSTILEPLAYERS-CanBeSieged,GTE,1</Req>
                     <Target>LOC,RADIUS,1</Target>
